# Nord Names

**[Names](Lore_Names.md)**
[Altmer](Lore_Altmer_Names.md) — [Argonian](Lore_Argonian_Names.md) — [Bosmer](Lore_Bosmer_Names.md) — [Breton](Lore_Breton_Names.md) — [Daedra](Lore_Daedra_Names.md) — [Dunmer](Lore_Dunmer_Names.md) — [Imperial](Lore_Imperial_Names.md) — [Khajiit](Lore_Khajiit_Names.md) — [Maormer](Lore_Maormer_Names.md) — Nord — [Orc](Lore_Orc_Names.md) — [Reachman](Lore_Reachman_Names.md) — [Redguard](Lore_Redguard_Names.md)
---
This is a list of all the known **[Nord](Lore_Nord.md) names**, compiled from the games by frequency.

## Male Nord Names

### Arena
[Thelen](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Arena:Thelen_Kaarn)

### [Arena](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Arena:Arena) and [Daggerfall](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Daggerfall:Daggerfall)
- Given names for male Nord in Arena and Daggerfall seem to consist of one of thirteen prefixes and one of thirteen suffixes.
- The 13 prefixes for male Nord names are: Al, Asg, Bj, Er, Fenr, Har, Ingm, Jurg, Kj, Moj, Sor, Torb, Ulr
- The 13 suffixes for male Nord names are: ald, an, ar, arik, arke, arne, eld, en, ens, er, ik, is, orn

**Therefore, all of the male Nord names in Arena and Daggerfall are:**

| Alald, | Alan, | Alar, | Alarik, | Alarke, | Alarne, | Aleld, | Alen, | Alens, | Aler, | Alik, | Alis, | Alorn, |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Asgald, | Asgan, | Asgar, | Asgarik, | Asgarke, | Asgarne, | Asgeld, | Asgen, | Asgens, | Asger, | Asgik, | Asgis, | Asgorn, |
| Bjald, | Bjan, | Bjar, | Bjarik, | Bjarke, | Bjarne, | Bjeld, | Bjen, | Bjens, | Bjer, | Bjik, | Bjis, | Bjorn, |
| Erald, | Eran, | Erar, | Erarik, | Erarke, | Erarne, | Ereld, | Eren, | Erens, | Erer, | Erik, | Eris, | Erorn, |
| Fenrald, | Fenran, | Fenrar, | Fenrarik, | Fenrarke, | Fenrarne, | Fenreld, | Fenren, | Fenrens, | Fenrer, | Fenrik, | Fenris, | Fenrorn, |
| Harald, | Haran, | Harar, | Hararik, | Hararke, | Hararne, | Hareld, | Haren, | Harens, | Harer, | Harik, | Haris, | Harorn, |
| Ingmald, | Ingman, | Ingmar, | Ingmarik, | Ingmarke, | Ingmarne, | Ingmeld, | Ingmen, | Ingmens, | Ingmer, | Ingmik, | Ingmis, | Ingmorn, |
| Jurgald, | Jurgan, | Jurgar, | Jurgarik, | Jurgarke, | Jurgarne, | Jurgeld, | Jurgen, | Jurgens, | Jurger, | Jurgik, | Jurgis, | Jurgorn, |
| Kjald, | Kjan, | Kjar, | Kjarik, | Kjarke, | Kjarne, | Kjeld, | Kjen, | Kjens, | Kjer, | Kjik, | Kjis, | Kjorn, |
| Mojald, | Mojan, | Mojar, | Mojarik, | Mojarke, | Mojarne, | Mojeld, | Mojen, | Mojens, | Mojer, | Mojik, | Mojis, | Mojorn, |
| Sorald, | Soran, | Sorar, | Sorarik, | Sorarke, | Sorarne, | Soreld, | Soren, | Sorens, | Sorer, | Sorik, | Soris, | Sororn, |
| Torbald, | Torban, | Torbar, | Torbarik, | Torbarke, | Torbarne, | Torbeld, | Torben, | Torbens, | Torber, | Torbik, | Torbis, | Torborn, |
| Ulrald, | Ulran, | Ulrar, | Ulrarik, | Ulrarke, | Ulrarne, | Ulreld, | Ulren, | Ulrens, | Ulrer, | Ulrik, | Ulris, | Ulrorn |

Whether this was a mistake or whether they were intended to have some back-story for this uncharacteristic name is impossible to guess, but the former is more likely given how inconsequential this character is in the game.

## Female Nord Names

### Arena and Daggerfall
- Given names for female Nords in Arena and Daggerfall seem to consist of one of thirteen prefixes and one of seven suffixes.
- The 13 prefixes for female Nord names are: An, Bet, Dor, Ell, Han, Hell, Ing, Jyt, Kirst, Met, Morg, Sill, Ull
- The 7 suffixes for female Nord names are: a, e, en, ia, ina, ne, te

**Therefore, all of the female Nord names in Arena and Daggerfall are:**

| Ana, | Ane, | Anen, | Ania, | Anina, | Anne, | Ante, |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Beta, | Bete, | Beten, | Betia, | Betina, | Betne, | Bette, |
| Dora, | Dore, | Doren, | Doria, | Dorina, | Dorne, | Dorte, |
| Ella, | Elle, | Ellen, | Ellia, | Ellina, | Ellne, | Ellte, |
| Hana, | Hane, | Hanen, | Hania, | Hanina, | Hanne, | Hante, |
| Hella, | Helle, | Hellen, | Hellia, | Hellina, | Hellne, | Hellte, |
| Inga, | Inge, | Ingen, | Ingia, | Ingina, | Ingne, | Ingte, |
| Jyta, | Jyte, | Jyten, | Jytia, | Jytina, | Jytne, | Jytte, |
| Kirsta, | Kirste, | Kirsten, | Kirstia, | Kirstina, | Kirstne, | Kirstte, |
| Meta, | Mete, | Meten, | Metia, | Metina, | Metne, | Mette, |
| Morga, | Morge, | Morgen, | Morgia, | Morgina, | Morgne, | Morgte, |
| Silla, | Sille, | Sillen, | Sillia, | Sillina, | Sillne, | Sillte, |
| Ulla, | Ulle, | Ullen, | Ullia, | Ullina, | Ullne, | Ullte |

### Lore

## Clan Names and Titles

### Patronymic Last Names
In *Arena* and *Daggerfall* all Nords male and female have a surname ending in *-sen* (meaning "son of"), but there are also other instances such as in a *Daggerfall* book and ESO where the feminine *-dottir* suffix is used (meaning "daughter of"). The *-sen* suffix being used both by males and females would indicate that the Nords of the time adopted [patronymic](https://www.wikipedia.org/wiki/Patronymic#Norse_languages) surnames as a cultural motif.

| #### Arena and Daggerfall <br> - Surnames for Nords in Arena and Daggerfall consist of the male prefixes and suffixes and ending in 'sen' <br> - The 13 prefixes for Nord names are: Al, Asg, Bj, Er, Fenr, Har, Ingm, Jurg, Kj, Moj, Sor, Torb, Ulr <br> - The 13 suffixes for Nord names are: ald, an, ar, arik, arke, arne, eld, en, ens, er, ik, is, orn <br> <br> **Therefore, all of the Nord surnames ### Compound Last Names
Starting with *Morrowind,* most Nords have no family name or patronym. Instead their last names typically consist of a compound or hyphenated compound name rendered in regular [Tamrielic (i.e. English)](Lore_Tamrielic.md). According to *[The Hope of the Redoran](Lore_The_Hope_of_the_Redoran.md)* book, noble Nordic families traditionally have omens read for their children where a compound name may be given to the child based on the omen.

| #### Morrowind <br> - Compound Names: <br> <br> [Farseer](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Haema_Farseer), [Highlander](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Hrondar_Highlander) <br> <br> - Hyphenated Names: <br> <br> **2x**: Half-Troll ([1](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Greidil_Half-Troll), [2](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Yngling_Half-Troll)), Hard-Heart ([1](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Radd_Hard-Heart), [2](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Sjoring_Hard-Heart)) <br> **1x**: [Blue-Tooth](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Roggvar_Blue-Tooth), [Deep-Raed](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Hisin_Deep-Raed), [Elf-Hewer](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Alfhedil_Elf-Hewer), [Fine-Hair](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Sold_Fine-Hair), [Fire-Eye](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Eydis_Fire-Eye), [Flat-Foot](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Hrisskar_Flat-Foot), [Fork-Beard](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Fanar_Fork-Beard), [Hairy-Breeks](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Godrod_Hairy-Breeks), [Hard-Mouth](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Onmi_Hard-Mouth), [Hearth-Healer](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Eiruki_Hearth-Healer), [Home-Wrecker](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Horstar_Home-Wrecker), [Horse-Mouth](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Sjorvar_Horse-Mouth), [Long-Leg](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Hlora_Long-Leg), [Red-tooth](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Morrowind:Hamlof_Red-tooth), ### Titles
Titles as suffixes are often hyphenated. Note that unlike clan names, titles may be changed over the course of one's lifetime, and there are a few incidents of single individuals with multiple titles at different times. Titles are typically added after or occasionally before a Nord's forename.

## Nord Skaal Names
These are the names of the [Skaal](Lore_Skaal.md), a tribe of Nords inhabiting [Solstheim](Lore_Solstheim.md).

### Male Skaal Names

#### Morrowind
[Aesliip](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Draugr_Lord_Aesliip), [Alvring](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Alvring_Whitebeard), [Andrelheim](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Andrelheim), [Bathmar](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bathmar_Bold-Lute), [Bronrod](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bronrod_the_Roarer), [Brynjolfr](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Brynjolfr), [Engar](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Engar_Ice-Mane), [Erich](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Erich_the_Unworthy), [Hagrad](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Hagrad_the_Stone), [Ingmar](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Ingmar), [Korst](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Korst_Wind-Eye), [Lassnr](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Lassnr), [Rigmor](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Rigmor_Halfhand), [Rolf](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Rolf_Long-Tooth), [Sattir](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Sattir_the_Bold), [Skjoldr](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Skjoldr_Wolf-Runner), [Snedbrir](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Snedbrir_the_Smith), [Tharsten](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Tharsten_Heart-Fang), [Tymvaul](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Bloodmoon:Tymvaul)

#### Skyrim
[Baldor](Skyrim_Baldor_Iron-Shaper.md), [Deor](Skyrim_Deor_Woodcutter.md), [Elmus](Skyrim_Elmus.md), [Halbarn](Skyrim_Halbarn_Iron-Fur.md), [Kuvar](Skyrim_Kuvar.md), [Nikulas](Skyrim_Nikulas_(Dragonborn).md), [Oslaf](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf), [Sirkjorg](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Sirkjorg), [Storn](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider), [Tharstan](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Tharstan), [Torkild](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild), [Wulf](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood)
